***изнемогать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнемогать.html>изнемога́ть</a> (15510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изнемо́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznemóg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнемогать.html>изнемога́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznemogátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнемочь.html>изнемо́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be exhausted <i>(by)</i>, to break down <i>(with)</i>, to grow faint <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изнемогать.html>изнемога́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жары́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>iznemogájet</b> ot žarý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the heat has exhausted him; he can't stand/bear the heat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изнемогать.html>изнемога́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:усталость.html>уста́лости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>iznemogájet</b> ot ustálosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is dead tired; he is dead beat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изнемогать.html>изнемога́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жестью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>iznemogátʹ</b> pod tjážestʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to grow faint under a weight</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:износить.html>износи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изношенный.html>изно́шенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznóšennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>worn-out, threadbare, shabby
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изношенный.html>изно́шенный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:организм.html>органи́зм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>iznóšennyj</b> organízm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">worn [prematurely aged] organism</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изношенный.html>изно́шенный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:костюм.html>костю́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>iznóšennyj</b> kostjúm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">threadbare/shabby suit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>depreciated</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнурять.html>изнуря́вший</a> (23779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнурять.html>изнуря́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznurjávšij</span>)

***изнурять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнурять.html>изнуря́ть</a> (23779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изнури́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнурять.html>изнуря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznurjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изнури́ть</b>)

***изнывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнывать.html>изныва́ть</a> (17214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изны́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнывать.html>изныва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изны́ть</b>)

<li>to be bored to death</li></ol>

***изо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>изо́</a> (1979)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ízo</span>) <i>+ genitive case</i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ízo</b> dnja v denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">day by day; day after day; from day to day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ízo</b> vsej síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with might and main; with all one’s strength</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>изо́</a></b> is used before some awkward consonant clusters, such as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>изо́</a> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vsex</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>. In most cases, use <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> instead.</li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:описание.html>описа́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a> какого-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объе́кта</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:относительно.html>относи́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:некий.html>не́коего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:контейнер.html>конте́йнера</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>нахо́дится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внутри.html>внутри́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:контейнер.html>конте́йнера</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительно.html>сравни́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:центр.html>це́нтру</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конечный.html>коне́чная</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вне.html>вне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:контейнер.html>конте́йнера</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительно.html>сравни́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:центр.html>це́нтра</a></i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обилие.html>оби́лие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obílije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобилие.html>изоби́лие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobílije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобилие.html>изоби́лия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобилие.html>изоби́лия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобилие.html>изоби́лий</a></b>)

<ol><li>abundance, plenty, profusion, multitude, wealth, plethora

***изобиловать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изобиловать.html>изоби́ловать</a> (21744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобиловать.html>изоби́ловать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobílovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to abound, to bristle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be plentiful</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to teem</li>
<li>to flow</li>
<li>to roll in</li>
<li>to be replete</li></ol>

***изображавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изображаться.html>изобража́вшийся</a> (21810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изображаться.html>изобража́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobražávšijsja</span>)
</p>

***изобразить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изобразить.html>изобрази́ть</a> (3359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобразить.html>изобрази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobrazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изображать.html>изобража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to depict, to picture, to portray
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">а́льфред хичко́к <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изобразить.html>изобрази́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужасный.html>ужа́сную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:натура.html>нату́ру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льмах</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Álʹfrɛd Xičkók <b>izobrazíl</b> užásnuju natúru ljudéj v svoíx fílʹmax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Alfred Hitchcock depicted the horrible nature of people in his films.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to describe; to represent, to paint</li>
<li>to imitate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изображение.html>изображе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izobražénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобразиться.html>изобрази́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobrazítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изображаться.html>изобража́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лице́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изобразиться.html>изобрази́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nejó na licé <b>izobrazílsja</b> ispúg.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Her face <b>expressed</b> fear.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобразить.html>изобрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izobrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрести.html>обрести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obrestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобрести.html>изобрести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izobrestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изобретать.html>изобрета́ть</a></b>)
